   return candidates\n   604→\n   605→\n   606→def _save_candidates_to_db(db_manager, candidates: List[CandidateBasic], source_search: str) -> None:\n   607→    \"\"\"\n   608→    Save or update 676→\n   677→\n   678→async def _click_avatar_for_profile_url(page: Page, name: str, company: str) -> Optional[str]:\n   679→    \"\"\"Click a candidate's avatar/name on the current search results page to get their profile URL.\n   680→\n   681→    Finds the candidate card matching name (and optionally company), clicks the\n   682→    avatar or name element, waits for navigation to the profile page, and returns\n   683→    the full profile URL.\n   684→\n   685→    Args:\n   686→        page: Playwright page on the search results\n   687→        name: Candidate name to match\n   688→        company: Candidate company to help disambiguate\n   689→\n   690→    Returns:\n   691→        Profile URL string, or None if not found\n   692→    \"\"\"\n   693→    try:\n   694→        # Use JS to find the index of the matching avatar image\n   695→        avatar_index = await page.evaluate('''(args) => {\n   696→            const { name, company } = args;\n   697→            const images = document.querySelectorAll('img');\n   698→            let idx = 0;\n   699→\n   700→            for (const img of images) {\n   701→                const rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();\n   702→                if (rect.width > 100 || rect.height > 100) continue;\n   703→                if (rect.width < 20 || rect.height < 20) continue;\n   704→\n   705→                // Find parent card\n   706→                let card = img.parentElement;\n   707→                for (let i = 0; i < 8 && card; i++) {\n   708→                    const cardRect = card.getBoundingClientRect();\n   709→                    if (cardRect.width > 200 && cardRect.height > 50 && cardRect.height < 200) {\n   710→                        break;\n   711→                    }\n   712→                    card = card.parentElement;\n   713→                }\n   714→                if (!card) { idx++; continue; }\n   715→\n   716→                const cardText = card.textContent || '';\n   717→                if (!cardText.includes(name)) { idx++; continue; }\n   718→                if (company && !cardText.includes(company)) { idx++; continue; }\n   719→\n   720→                // Return the index among all avatar-sized images\n   721→                return idx;\n   722→            }\n   723→            return -1;\n   724→        }''', {'name': name, 'company': company})\n   725→\n   726→        if avatar_index < 0:\n   727→            logger.debug(f\"Avatar not found on page for '{name}'\")\n   728→            return None\n   729→\n   730→        # Click the avatar image at the found index\n   731→        # Re-select all avatar-sized images and click the one at avatar_index\n   732→        clicked = await page.evaluate('''(idx) => {\n   733→            const images = document.querySelectorAll('img');\n   734→            let count = 0;\n   735→            for (const img of images) {\n   736→                const rect = img.getBoundingClientRect();\n   737→                if (rect.width > 100 || rect.height > 100) continue;\n   738→                if (rect.width < 20 || rect.height < 20) continue;\n   739→                if (count === idx) {\n   740→                    // Try to find a clickable parent <a>\n   741→                    let el = img;\n   742→                    while (el) {\n   743→                        if (el.tagName === 'A' && el.href) {\n   744→                            el.click();\n   745→                            return true;\n   746→                        }\n   747→                        el = el.parentElement;\n   748→                    }\n   749→                    // No <a> found, click the image directly\n   750→                    img.click();\n   751→                    return true;\n   752→                }\n   753→                count++;\n   754→            }\n   755→            return false;\n   756→        }''', avatar_index)\n   757→\n   758→        if not clicked:\n   759→            logger.debug(f\"Could not              lambda url: '/profile/detail' in url or 'dstu=' in url,\n   766→                timeout=8000,\n   767→            )\n   768→        except Exception:\n   769→            # URL might not change if it opens in a new tab or overlay\n   770→            await page.wait_for_timeout(2000)\n   771→\n   772→        current_url = page.url\n   773→        if '/profile/detail' in current_url or 'dstu=' in current_url:\n   774→            logger.info(f\"Navigated to profile for '{name}': {current_url}\")\n   775→            return current_url\n   776→\n   777→        logger.debug(f\"Clicked avatar but did not land on profile page: {current_url}\")\n   778→        return None\n   779→\n   780→    except Exception as e:\n   781→        logger.debug(f\"_click_avatar_for_profile_url error for '{name}': {e}\")\n   782→        return None\n   783→\n   784→\n   785→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   786→# Enterprise recruitment path (Path \"ent/talents/discover\"\n   791→\n   792→\n   793→async def search_candidates_enterprise(\n   794→    keywords: str,\n   795→    company: Optional[tuple] = None,\n   796→    pages: int = 1,\n   797→    browser: Optional[BrowserManager] = None,\n   798→    keep_tab_open: bool = False,\n   799→) -> List[CandidateBasic]:\n   800→    \"\"\"Search for candidates via the enterprise recruitment path.\n   801→\n   802→    Flow:\n   803→    1. Switch to primary tab -> navigate to homepage -> click \"招聘\" tab (opens new tab)\n   804→    2. Wait for enterprise page to load\n   805→    3. Add keyword filter -> submit\n   806→    4. Optionally add company filter\n   807→    5. Extract candidates from enterprise card layout\n   808→    6. For additional pages, scroll to trigger infinite scroll\n   809→    7. Close enterprise tab unless keep_tab_open is True\n   810→\n   811→    Args:\n   812→        keywords: Search keywords\n   813→        company: Filter by company names (optional)\n   814→        pages: Number of scroll-pages to extract\n   815→        browser: Browser manager instance\n   816→        keep_tab_open: If True, leave enterprise tab open (for inline messaging)\n   817→\n   818→    Returns:\n   819→        List of CandidateBasic objects\n   820→    \"\"\"\n   821→    validate_keywords(keywords)\n   822→\n   823→    if browser is None:\n   824→        browser = get_browser_manager()\n   825→\n   826→    config = get_config()\n   827→    rate_limiter = get_rate_limiter()\n   828→    db_manager = get_db_manager()\n   829→\n   830→    await ensure_logged_in(browser)\n   831→\n   832→    all_candidates: List[CandidateBasic] = []\n   833→    enterprise_tab_opened = False\n   834→\n   835→    with Progress(\n   836→        SpinnerColumn(),\n   837→        TextColumn(\"[progress.description]{task.description}\"),\n   838→        console=console,\n   839→    ) as progress:\n   840→        task = progress.add_task(\"Opening enterprise recruitment...\", total=None)\n   841→\n   842→        try:\n   843→            await async_check_rate_limit(\"search\")\n   844→\n   845→            # Always start from the primary tab to avoid navigating user's open content\n   846→            browser.switch_to_primary_tab()\n   847→            page = browser.page\n   848→\n   849→            # Step 1: Navigate to homepage and click 招聘 tab\n   850→            await retry_navigation(page, MAIMAI_HOME_URL, wait_until=\"domcontentloaded\")\n   851→            await async_random_delay(\"page_load\")\n   852→\n   853→            sel = config.get_selector(\"enterprise.recruitment_tab\")\n   854→            recruitment_tab = await page.wait_for_selector(sel, timeout=5000)\n   855→            if not recruitment_tab:\n   856→                raise SelectorNotFoundError(f\"Could not find recruitment tab: {sel}\")\n   857→\n   858→            # Click opens a new tab — use BrowserManager API\n   859→            await recruitment_tab.click()\n   860→            page = await browser.wait_for_new_tab(timeout=15000)\n   861→            enterprise_tab_opened = True\n   862→\n   863→            progress.update(task, description=\"Enterprise page loaded\")\n   864→\n   865→            # Wait for the enterprise page URL\n   866→            try:\n   867→                await page.wait_for_url(\n   868→                    lambda url: ENTERPRISE_URL_MARKER in url,\n   869→                    timeout=15000,\n   870→                )\n   871→            except Exception:\n   872→                logger.warning(f\"Enterprise URL marker not found, current URL: {page.url}\")\n   873→\n   874→            await async_random_delay(\"action\")\n   875→\n   876→            # Step 2: Add keyword\n   877→            progress.update(task, description=f\"Adding keyword: {keywords}\")\n   878→\n   879→            add_kw_sel = config.get_selector(\"enterprise.add_keyword_button\")\n   880→            add_kw_btn = await page.wait_for_selector(add_kw_sel, timeout=5000)\n   881→            if add_kw_btn:\n   882→                await add_kw_btn.click()\n   883→                await async_random_delay(\"action\")\n   884→\n   885→            kw_input_sel = config.get_selector(\"enterprise.keyword_input\")\n   886→            await page.wait_for_selector(kw_input_sel, timeout=5000)\n   887→            await human_type(page, kw_input_sel, keywords)\n   888→            await async_random_delay(\"action\")\n   889→\n   890→            kw_submit_sel = config.get_selector(\"enterprise.keyword_submit\")\n   891→            submit_btn = await page.wait_for_selector(kw_submit_sel, timeout=3000)\n   892→            if submit_btn:\n   893→                await submit_btn.click()\n   894→                await async_random_delay(\"page_load\")\n   895→\n   896→            # Step 3: Add company filter if specified\n   897→            if company:\n   898→                progress.update(task, description=\"Adding company filter...\")\n   899→                add_co_sel = config.get_selector(\"enterprise.add_company_button\")\n   900→                add_co_btn = await page.wait_for_selector(add_co_sel, timeout=5000)\n   901→                if add_co_btn:\n   902→                    await add_co_btn.click()\n   903→                    await async_random_delay(\"action\")\n   904→\n   905→                co_input_sel = config.get_selector(\"enterprise.company_input\")\n   906→                for co_name in company:\n   907→                    await page.wait_for_selector(co_input_sel, timeout=5000)\n   908→                    await human_type(page, co_input_sel, co_name)\n   909→                    await async_random_delay(\"action\")\n   910→\n   911→                    # Click suggestion dropdown item\n   912→                    try:\n   913→                        suggestion = await page.wait_for_selector(\n   914→                            f\"text='{co_name}'\", timeout=3000\n   915→                        )\n   916→                        if suggestion:\n   917→                            await suggestion.click()\n   918→                            await async_random_delay(\"action\")\n   919→                    except Exception:\n   920→                        logger.debug(f\"Company suggestion not found for: {co_name}\")\n   921→\n   922→            # Step 4: Wait for results and extract\n   923→            await page.wait_for_timeout(3000)\n   924→            await check_captcha(page, report_to_rate_limiter=True)\n   925→\n   926→            for page_num in range(1, pages + 1):\n   927→                progress.update(task, description=f\"Extracting page {page_num}/{pages}...\")\n   928→\n   929→                candidates = await _extract_enterprise_results(page)\n   930→\n   931→                if not candidates:\n   932→                    logger.info(f\"No enterprise results on page {page_num}\")\n   933→                    break\n   934→\n   935→                # Filter non-R&D roles\n   936→                before_filter = len(candidates)\n   937→                candidates = [c for c in candidates if not _is_non_rd_title(c.title)]\n   938→                filtered = before_filter - len(candidates)\n   939→                if filtered > 0:\n   940→                    logger.info(f\"Filtered out {filtered} non-R&D candidates\")\n   941→\n   942→                all_candidates.extend(candidates)\n   943→                progress.update(task, description=f\"Page {page_num}: Found {len(candidates)} candidates\")\n   944→\n   945→                rate_limiter.log_action(\"search\", {\n   946→                    \"keywords\": keywords,\n   947→                    \"page\": page_num,\n   948→                    \"results\": len(candidates),\n   949→                    \"mode\": \"enterprise\",\n   950→                })\n   951→\n   952→                _save_candidates_to_db(db_manager, candidates, keywords)\n   953→\n   954→                # Scroll for next page (infinite scroll)\n   955→                if page_num < pages:\n   956→                    await human_scroll(page, \"down\", distance=800)\n   957→                    await async_random_delay(\"page_load\")\n   958→                    await page.wait_for_timeout(2000)\n   959→\n   960→        except Exception as e:\n   961→            logger.error(f\"Enterprise search error: {e}\")\n   962→            await browser.screenshot(\"enterprise_search_error\")\n   963→            progress.update(task, description=f\"Error: {str(e)[:40]}\")\n   964→        finally:\n   965→            # Found {len(all_candidates)} candidates.[/green]\")\n   975→    return all_candidates\n   976→\n   977→\n   978→async def _extract_enterprise_results(page: Page) -> List[CandidateBasic]:\n   979→    \"\"\"Extract candidate information from enterprise recruitment results page.\n   980→\n   981→    The enterprise UI has a different card layout from search_center.\n   982→    Uses JS-based extraction tailored to the enterprise talent cards.\n   983→\n   984→    Args:\n   985→        page: Playwright page instance on the enterprise results page\n   986→\n   987→    Returns:\n   988→        List of CandidateBasic objects\n   989→    \"\"\"\n   990→    candidates = []\n   991→\n   992→    try:\n   993→        await page.wait_for_load_state(\"networkidle\", timeout=10000)\n   994→           '[class*=\"talent-item\"]',\n  1009→                '[class*=\"card-wrap\"]',\n  1010→            ];\n  1011→\n  1012→            let cards = [];\n  1013→            for (const sel of cardSelectors) {\n  1014→                cards = document.querySelectorAll(sel);\n  1015→                if (cards.length > 0) break;\n  1016→            }\n  1017→\n  1018→            // Fallback: find cards by avatar image pattern (same as search_center)\n  1019→            if (cards.length === 0) {\n  1020→                const images = document.querySelectorAll('img');\n  1021→ 100 || rect.height > 100) continue;\n  1026→                    if (rect.width < 30 || rect.height < 30) continue;\n  1027→\n  1028→                    let card = img.parentElement;\n  1029→       template = config.get_template(template_name)\n   383→    except Exception:\n   384→        raise ValidationError(f\"Template not found: {template_name}\")\n   385→\n   386→    # Create shared 464→    )\n   465→\n   466→    if not confirm:\n   467→        console.print(\"[yellow]Batch send cancelled.[/yellow]\")\n   468→        return results\n   469→\n   470→    # Send messages one by        task = progress.add_task(\"Sending messages...\", total=len(send_list))\n   480→\n   481→        max_retries = 2\n   482→        rate_limit_hit = False\n   483→\n   484→        for c in      await async_check_rate_limit('send_message')\n   491→            except RateLimitExceededError as e:\n   492→                console.print(f\"\\n[yellow]Rate limit reached: {e}[/yellow]\")\n   493→                remaining = len(send_list) - (results['sent'] + results['failed'])\n   494→                results['rate_limited'] = remaining\n   495→                results['details'].append({\n 585→    Render template with variables.\n   586→\n   587→    Variable values are HTML-entity-escaped to prevent injection if the\n   588→    platform renders messages as HTML.\n   589→\n   590→    Args:\n   591→        template_content: Template string with {variable} placeholders\n   592→        variables: Variable values to substitute\n   593→\n   594→    Returns:\n   595→        Rendered _find_element_by_selectors(page: Page, selectors: List[str], timeout: int = 3000):\n   745→    \"\"\"Try multiple selectors and return the first matching element.\n   746→\n   747→    Args:\n   748→ 873→\n   874→\n   875→async def _click_send_button(page: Page, config) -> bool:\n   876→    \"\"\"Find and click send button.\"\"\"\n   877→    selectors = [\n   878→ 898→    \"\"\"\n   899→    Verify that a message was actually sent by checking the conversation area.\n   900→\n   901→    Polls up to `timeout` ms with short intervals to handle async rendering.\n   902→\n   903→    Checks for:\n   904→    1. The sent message content appearing in the conversation\n   905→    2. The message input being cleared (indicating successful send)\n   906→    3. A sent/delivered indicator element\n   907→\n   908→    Args:\n   909→        page: Playwright page instance\n   910→        content: The message content that was sent\n   911→        timeout: Max time to wait for verification in ms\n   912→\n   913→    Returns:\n   914→        True if message send was verified\n   915→    \"\"\"\n   916→    import asyncio\n   917→    import time\n   918→\n   919→    # Short snippet for matching (first 20 chars, avoid template artifacts)\n   920→    snippet = content[:20].strip()\n   921→\n   922→    poll_interval_ms = 500\n   923→    deadline = time.monotonic() + timeout / 1000.0\n   924→\n   925→    while True:\n   926→        try:\n   927→            # Strategy 1: Check if message content appears in conversation area\n   928→            verified = await page.evaluate('''(snippet) => {\n   929→                const chatSelectors = [\n   930→                    '[class*=\"message-list\"]',\n   931→                    '[class*=\"chat-content\"]',\n   932→                    '[class*=\"conversation\"]',\n   933→                    '[class*=\"msg-list\"]',\n   934→                    '[class*=\"im-message\"]',\n   935→                    '[class*=\"chat-msg\"]',\n   936→                ];\n   937→\n   938→                for (const sel of chatSelectors) {\n   939→                    const container = document.querySelector(sel);\n   940→                    if (container && container.textContent.includes(snippet)) {\n   941→                        return true;\n   942→                    }\n   943→                }\n   944→\n   945→                // Fallback: scan leaf-ish elements in the lower portion of the page\n   946→                const viewportHeight = window.innerHeight;\n   947→                const elements = document.querySelectorAll('div, p, span');\n   948→                for (const el of elements) {\n   949→                    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();\n   950→                    if (rect.top > viewportHeight * 0.3 && el.textContent.includes(snippet)) {\n   951→                        if (el.textContent.length < snippet.length + 200) {\n   952→                            return true;\n   953→                        }\n   954→                    }\n   955→                }\n   956→\n   957→                return false;\n   958→            }''', snippet)\n   959→\n   960→            if verified:\n   961→                logger.debug(\"Message send verified: content found in conversation\")\n   962→                return True\n   963→\n   964→            # Strategy 2: Check if input was cleared (indicates successful send)\n   965→            input_cleared = await page.evaluate('''() => {\n   966→                const inputs = document.querySelectorAll(\n   967→                    'textarea, [contenteditable=\"true\"], input[type=\"text\"]'\n   968→                );\n   969→                for (const input of inputs) {\n   970→                    const rect = input.getBoundingClientRect();\n   971→                    if (rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0) {\n   972→                        const value = input.value || input.textContent || '';\n   973→                        if (value.trim() === '') {\n   974→                            return true;\n   975→                        }\n   976→                    }\n   977→                }\n   978→                return false;\n   979→            }''')\n   980→\n   981→            if input_cleared:\n   982→                logger.debug(\"Message send verified: input field was cleared\")\n   983→                return True\n   984→\n   985→            # Strategy 3: Check for sent/delivered indicators\n   986→            sent_indicators = [\n   987→
